  AUTHORS   Shimomura,Y., Aoki,N., Schweizer,J., Langbein,L., Rogers,M.A.,
            Winter,H. and Ito,M.
  TITLE     Polymorphisms in the human high sulfur hair keratin-associated
            protein 1, KAP1, gene family
  JOURNAL   J. Biol. Chem. 277 (47), 45493-45501 (2002)
   PUBMED   12228244
REFERENCE   2  (bases 1 to 556)
  AUTHORS   Shimomura,Y.
  TITLE     Direct Submission
  JOURNAL   Submitted (11-MAR-2002) Contact:Yutaka Shimomura Niigata University
            School of Medicine, Department of Dermatology; Asahimachi-dori,
            Niigata, Niigata 951-8510, Japan
COMMENT     We have identified several size polymorphisms of hKAP1.3 gene
            during the analysis of hKAP1 genes using the genomic DNAs from 100
            Japanese and 100 Caucasian controls. hKAP1.9 has been detected in
            only one Caucasian control. Comparisons of nucleotide sequence
            between hKAP1.3 and hKAP1.9 revealed complete sequence identity
            except for a 78 nucleotides deletion in the coding region of
            hKAP1.9. These data indicate that hKAP1.9 is a rare size
            polymorphism of hKAP1.3 gene.
